<h1 _ngcontent-opu-c119="" class="doc-title ng-star-inserted" title="@ohos.pasteboard (剪贴板)"> @ohos.pasteboard (剪贴板) </h1>

<div _ngcontent-opu-c106="" auitextselectionexpansion="" class="markdown-body ng-star-inserted renderOptimization" style="position: relative;">   <div>    <p>本模块提供管理系统剪贴板的能力，支持系统复制、粘贴功能。系统剪贴板支持对文本、HTML、URI、Want、PixelMap等内容的操作。</p>    <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">      <p>本模块首批接口从API version 6开始支持。后续版本的新增接口，采用上角标单独标记接口的起始版本。</p>     </div></div></div>    <div class="tiledSection scroll-inwindow" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 247px;">     <h2 id="导入模块" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">导入模块<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="导入模块" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><div _ngcontent-opu-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-opu-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-opu-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-opu-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-opu-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-opu-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-opu-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-opu-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-opu-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-opu-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-opu-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="ts prettyprint linenums hljs language-typescript" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> { pasteboard } <span class="hljs-keyword">from</span> <span class="hljs-string">'@kit.BasicServicesKit'</span>;</li></ol></pre></div></div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection scroll-inwindow" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 870px;">     <h2 id="常量" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">常量<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="常量" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.MiscServices.Pasteboard</p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.4.4.1.5.1.1" width="25%">名称</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.4.4.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.4.4.1.5.1.3" width="25%">值</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.4.4.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">MAX_RECORD_NUM<sup>7+</sup></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">number</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">-</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>API version 10之前，此常量值为512，表示单个PasteData中所能包含的最大条目数为512。当剪贴板内容中添加的条目达到数量上限512后，后续的添加操作无效。</p>          <p>从API version 10开始，不再限制单个PasteData中所能包含的最大条目数。</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">MIMETYPE_TEXT_HTML<sup>7+</sup></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">string</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">'text/html'</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">HTML内容的MIME类型定义。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">MIMETYPE_TEXT_WANT<sup>7+</sup></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">string</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">'text/want'</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">Want内容的MIME类型定义。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">MIMETYPE_TEXT_PLAIN<sup>7+</sup></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">string</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">'text/plain'</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">纯文本内容的MIME类型定义。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">MIMETYPE_TEXT_URI<sup>7+</sup></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">string</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">'text/uri'</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">URI内容的MIME类型定义。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">MIMETYPE_PIXELMAP<sup>9+</sup></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">string</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">'pixelMap'</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">PixelMap内容的MIME类型定义。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection scroll-inwindow" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 614px;">     <h2 id="valuetype9" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">ValueType<sup>9+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="valuetype9" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>type ValueType = string | image.PixelMap | Want | ArrayBuffer</p>     <p>用于表示允许的数据字段类型。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.MiscServices.Pasteboard</p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t">                      <tbody><tr class="firstRow">         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.5.6.1.3.1.1" width="50%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.5.6.1.3.1.2" width="50%">说明</th>        </tr><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">string</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">表示string的类型。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">image.PixelMap</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">表示<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/arkts-apis-image-pixelmap">image.PixelMap</a>的类型。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">Want</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">表示<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-app-ability-want">Want</a>的类型。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">ArrayBuffer</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">表示ArrayBuffer的类型。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection scroll-inwindow" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1517px;">     <h2 id="pasteboardcreatedata9" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">pasteboard.createData<sup>9+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="pasteboardcreatedata9" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>createData(mimeType: string, value: ValueType): PasteData</p>     <p>构建一个指定类型的剪贴板内容对象。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.MiscServices.Pasteboard</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.6.7.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.6.7.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.6.7.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.6.7.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">mimeType</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">string</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">剪贴板数据对应的MIME类型，可以是<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-pasteboard#常量">常量</a>中已定义的类型，包括HTML类型，WANT类型，纯文本类型，URI类型，PIXELMAP类型；也可以是自定义的MIME类型，开发者可自定义此参数值, mimeType长度不能超过1024字节。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">value</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-pasteboard#valuetype9">ValueType</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">自定义数据内容。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>返回值：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t">                      <tbody><tr class="firstRow">         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.6.9.1.3.1.1" width="50%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.6.9.1.3.1.2" width="50%">说明</th>        </tr><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-pasteboard#pastedata">PasteData</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">剪贴板内容对象。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>错误码：</strong></p>     <p>以下错误码的详细介绍请参见<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/errorcode-universal">通用错误码</a>。</p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t">                      <tbody><tr class="firstRow">         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.6.12.1.3.1.1" width="50%">错误码ID</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.6.12.1.3.1.2" width="50%">错误信息</th>        </tr><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">401</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">Possible causes: 1. Mandatory parameters are left unspecified; 2. Incorrect parameters types; 3. Parameter verification failed.</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>示例1：</strong></p>     <div _ngcontent-opu-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">pasteboard.createData<sup>14+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="pasteboardcreatedata14" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>createData(data: Record&lt;string, ValueType&gt;): PasteData</p>     <p>构建一个包含多个类型数据的剪贴板内容对象。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.MiscServices.Pasteboard</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.7.6.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.7.6.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.7.6.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.7.6.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">data</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/introduction-to-arkts#对象字面量" target="_blank">Record</a>&lt;string, <a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-pasteboard#valuetype9">ValueType</a>&gt;</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>Record的key为剪贴板数据对应的MIME类型。可以是<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-pasteboard#常量">常量</a>中已定义的类型，包括HTML类型，WANT类型，纯文本类型，URI类型，PIXELMAP类型。也可以是自定义的MIME类型，可自定义此参数值，mimeType长度不能超过1024字节。</p>          <p>Record的value为key中指定MIME类型对应的数据。</p>          <p>Record中的首个key-value指定的MIME类型，会作为剪贴板内容对象中首个PasteDataRecord的默认MIME类型，非默认类型的数据在粘贴时只能使用<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-pasteboard#getdata14">getData</a>接口读取。</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>返回值：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t">                      <tbody><tr class="firstRow">         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.7.8.1.3.1.1" width="50%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.7.8.1.3.1.2" width="50%">说明</th>        </tr><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-pasteboard#pastedata">PasteData</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">剪贴板内容对象。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>错误码：</strong></p>     <p>以下错误码的详细介绍请参见<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/errorcode-universal">通用错误码</a>。</p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t">                      <tbody><tr class="firstRow">         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.7.11.1.3.1.1" width="50%">错误码ID</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.7.11.1.3.1.2" width="50%">错误信息</th>        </tr><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">401</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">Possible causes: 1. Mandatory parameters are left unspecified; 2. Incorrect parameters types; 3. Parameter verification failed.</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>示例1：</strong></p>     <div _ngcontent-opu-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div <div _ngcontent-opu-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-opu-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-opu-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-opu-c106="" <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.MiscServices.Pasteboard</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1375px;">     <h3 id="cancel15" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv" class="firsth2">cancel<sup>15+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="cancel15" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 15开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.MiscServices.Pasteboard</p>     <p><strong>示例：</strong></p>     <div device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">GetDataParams<sup>15+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="getdataparams15" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>应用在使用剪贴板提供的文件拷贝能力的情况下需要的参数，包含目标路径、文件冲突选项、进度条类型等。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 15开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.MiscServices.Pasteboard</p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%"><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-pasteboard#progresslistener15">ProgressListener</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder"       <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">progressSignal</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%"><a    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 206px;">     <h2 id="pastedatarecord7" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">PasteDataRecord<sup>7+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="pastedatarecord7" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>对于剪贴板中内容记录的抽象定义，称之为条目。剪贴板内容部分由一个或者多个条目构成，例如一条文本内容、一份HTML、一个URI或者一个Want。</p>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 603px;">     <h3 id="属性" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv" class="firsth2">属性<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 698px;">     <h3 id="toplaintext9" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">toPlainText<sup>9+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="toplaintext9" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>toPlainText(): string</p>     <p>将一个PasteDataRecord中的html、plain、uri内容强制转换为文本内容。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.MiscServices.Pasteboard</p>     <p><strong>返回值：</strong></p>     <div device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">addEntry<sup>14+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="addentry14" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>addEntry(type: string, value: ValueType): void</p>     <p>往一个PasteDataRecord中额外添加一种样式的自定义数据。此方式添加的MIME类型都不是Record的默认类型，粘贴时只能使用<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-pasteboard#getdata14">getData</a>接口读取对应数据。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.MiscServices.Pasteboard</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.30.6.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.30.6.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.30.6.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.30.6.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">type</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">string</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">剪贴板数据对应的MIME类型，可以是<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-pasteboard#常量">常量</a>中已定义的类型，包括HTML类型，WANT类型，纯文本类型，URI类型，PIXELMAP类型；也可以是自定义的MIME类型，开发者可自定义此参数值，mimeType长度不能超过1024字节。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">value</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-pasteboard#valuetype9">ValueType</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">自定义数据内容。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>错误码：</strong></p>     <p>以下错误码的详细介绍请参见<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/errorcode-universal">通用错误码</a>和见<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/errorcode-pasteboard">剪贴板错误码</a>。</p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t"> Mandatory parameters are left unspecified; 2. Incorrect parameters types; 3. Parameter verification failed.</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>示例：</strong></p>     <div _ngcontent-opu-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div id="converttotextdeprecated" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">convertToText<sup>(deprecated)</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">       <p>从 API version 7 开始支持，从 API version 9 开始废弃，建议使用<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-pasteboard#toplaintext9">toPlainText</a>替代。</p>      </div></div></div>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.MiscServices.Pasteboard</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.33.7.1.5.1.1" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.33.7.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">callback</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">AsyncCallback&lt;string&gt;</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">回调函数，当转换成功，err为undefined，data为强制转换的文本内容；否则返回错误信息。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>错误码：</strong></p>     <p>以下错误码的详细介绍请参见<a 'update', callback: () =&gt;void): void</p>     <p>订阅系统剪贴板内容变化事件，当系统剪贴板中内容变化时触发用户程序的回调。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.MiscServices.Pasteboard</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p> width="50%">说明</th>        </tr><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">Promise&lt;boolean&gt;</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">返回true表示系统剪贴板中有内容，返回false表示系统剪贴板中没有内容。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>示例：</strong></p>     <div _ngcontent-opu-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-opu-c106="" id="getdatawithprogress15" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">getDataWithProgress<sup>15+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">getChangeCount<sup>18+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="getchangecount18" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>getChangeCount(): number</p>     <p>获取剪贴板内容的变化次数。</p>     <p>执行成功时返回剪贴板内容的变化次数，否则返回0。</p>     <p>当剪贴板内容过期或调用<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-pasteboard#cleardatasync11">clearDataSync</a>等接口导致剪贴板内容为空时，内容变化次数不会因此改变。</p>     <p>系统重启或剪贴板服务异常重启时，剪贴板内容变化次数重新从0开始计数。对同一内容连续多次复制会被视作多次更改，每次复制均会导致内容变化次数增加。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 18开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.MiscServices.Pasteboard</p>     <p><strong>返回值：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t">                      <tbody><tr class="firstRow">         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.99.10.1.3.1.1" width="50%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.99.10.1.3.1.2" width="50%">说明</th>        </tr><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">number</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">返回读取到的剪贴板内容变化次数。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>示例：</strong></p>     <div _ngcontent-opu-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-opu-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-opu-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-opu-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-opu-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-opu-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-opu-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-opu-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-opu-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-opu-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-opu-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="ts prettyprint linenums hljs language-typescript" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-string">'@kit.BasicServicesKit'</span>;</li><li>
